wyth good seyn iuwes lyē ō lady son ihū crist whan ye seyne dedyn ye crosse sar • en trowen soo myche feith lyghtly cō uere whan men p̄chen hem • awe crist seȳ ten well lawe machemet shall faylen dothe lawe iawes cristꝭ lawe shal last wordis ende mā aske hem wheryn trowen yt saȳ god almaghty maker heuyn erth thingꝭ wythouten nothing doon day doine thing shalbe rewarid deseruyng thing sothe marchaunt egipte tyme crysten chapell side arabie wonned heremyte whan entred chapell yt litell hous lowe anon begā werē gret palays yate sarasins sayn yt furst myrakele machamet ded youthe aftir ward bygan machamet ben right wy gret astromyar sithē keper golde prince corydan gouerned ful wisly whan prynce dede weddid wife lady mē clepē quadryge machemet fell often falling euill wherfore ye lady wroth taken husband made beleue euer whan fell soo gabriel angel spake wyth gret bryghtnes angell fell downe machemet regned arabie yere lord vi cxx kynred ismael brahm̄ son begat agare chambirer therfore ye sare • ons ben clepid ismaelites agarens aga • ther bē clepid moabites sōme amonytis ij sōnes loth alsoo machemet loued wel holy man duellid wildirnes myle fro mount synay vale men goon fro arabie caldas dayes iurney fro see whan marchauntꝭ comē fro venys machamet went often mytage alle men wroth sothe wolde gladly heremet prieche made mē wakē nyght therfore thei wolde fayn haue heremet dede fell nyght machemet well dronken wyne fill slepe mē toke swerd shethe • e lay slepe slought ther heremet thē put vp age • shethe al blody morow whā founde heremyt dede hee wrothe wolde haue slayne men oō accorde said self slayne whan dronken▪ shewid swarde alle blody trowed sayd soth second myracle yt machamet dede cursed wyne alle dronkē wyne • sarasens yt ben deuout drynken noo
